The following principles should be recognised and enforced at EU level for the private copying exception: Private copying is justly accompanied by compensation for authors. Having levies on devices and media making private copies is an efficient and cost-effective way to organise the compensation. An important element of the system‚Äôs cost-effectiveness is to collect the levies at the earliest stages of the sales chain, i.e. from the manufacturer or the importer. The amount of private copying compensation should be linked to the value of the creative works being copied, not to the price ofthe devices which can depend on commercial strategies. The private copying system should be brought into the digital age taking into account that consumers make private copies more than ever before on ever more connected devices and services. There is a need for common principles for defining applicable levy rates and devices/services that should be subject to levies. ‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶. ‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶.

The following principles should be recognised and enforced at EU level for the private copying exception: Private copying is justly accompanied by compensation for authors. Having levies on devices and media making private copies is an efficient and cost-effective way to organise the compensation. An important element of the system‚Äôs cost-effectiveness is to collect the levies at the earliest stages of the sales chain, i.e. from the manufacturer or the importer. The amount of private copying compensation should be linked to the value of the creative works being copied, not to the price of the devices which can depend on commercial strategies. The private copying system should be brought into the digital age taking into account that consumers make private copies more than ever before on ever more connected devices and services. Thereis a need for common principles for defining applicable levy rates and devices/services that should be subject to levies. ‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶. ‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶.

De thuiskopiegelden vormeneen belangrijke bron van inkomsten voor rechthebbenden. Het is belangrijk dat in de voorstellen van de Europese Commissie, een effici√´nte en effectieve wijze van heffen van de thuiskopievergoeding in de digitale omgeving wordt bepleit. In het bijzonder moet de Europese Commissie bij haar voorstellen rekening houden met zo laag mogelijke administratieve lasten tussen de organisatie die in de desbetreffende lidstaat de heffing incasseert en de marktpartij die verantwoordelijk is voor de afdracht van de heffing. In de huidige situatie is dat de fabrikant dan wel de importeur van de desbetreffende drager, hetgeen een goede oplossing lijkt. Een Europees stelsel van thuiskopieheffing is complementair aan licensering. Deze twee moeten ook in de digitale omgeving naast elkaar blijven bestaan. ÔÇ NO‚ÄìPlease explain No need for further clarification. The scope and application of private copying and reprography exceptions is currently being clarified by the CJEU and at national level. We have a court case going on in Sweden, where Copyswede sued Sony Mobile for levies to be paid for smart phones (Sony Mobiles Walkman phones). The judgement is expected in late February 2104. The CJEU has confirmed that in those countries where consumers are allowed by law to make private copies of copyright protected content, rights holders have a right to be fairly compensated for these reproductions. The CJEU have made clear that levies should be calculated according to the assumed harm sustained by rights holders by the private copying in question. ÔÇ NO OPINION

De thuiskopiegelden vormen een belangrijke bron van inkomsten voor rechthebbenden. Het is belangrijk dat in de voorstellen van de Europese Commissie, een effici√´nte en effectieve wijze van heffen van de thuiskopievergoeding in de digitale omgeving wordt bepleit. In het bijzonder moet de Europese Commissie bij haar voorstellen rekening houden met zo laag mogelijke administratieve lasten tussen de organisatie die in de desbetreffende lidstaat de heffing incasseert en de marktpartij die verantwoordelijk is voor de afdracht van de heffing. In de huidige situatie is dat de fabrikant dan wel de importeur van de desbetreffende drager, hetgeen een goede oplossing lijkt. Een Europees stelsel van thuiskopieheffing is complementair aan licensering. Deze twee moeten ook in de digitale omgeving naast elkaar blijven bestaan. ‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶. ‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶.

ÔÇ NO OPINION 

In my opinion, DRM only prevents legitimate users and customers from accessing the content they have paid for. No DRM is going to be perfect, and they can all bebroken. As a result of this, anyillegally obtained content will inevitably be DRM free. Thanks to this,that content will be 100% usable, without restriction - exactly what the consumer wants. Conversely, legally obtained content comes with a large variety of restrictions - you never even own that content in any way (often only given the right to use a copy of it, less own, more lease). DRM in that past hasprevented me from accessing my own legal content - the most common issue with which is that the DRM fails to work as intended, blocking me from using the product I purchased, and often requiring me to install or use additional software and/or hardware that I otherwise didn't want or need. In the UK, it is only very recently that we have finally be given the legal right to rip and use mp3 versions of any CD purchased, for use on either our computer or mp3 player, something which most didn't realise was previously illegal, and which most had been doing anyway for years. This is still not true of anyvideo based media. ‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶. ‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶.

ÔÇ NO OPINION 

The following principles should be recognised and enforced at EU level for the private copying exception: Private copying is justly accompanied by compensation for authors. Having levies on devices and media making private copies is an efficient andcost-effective way to organise the compensation. An important element of the system‚Äôs cost-effectiveness is to collect the levies at the earliest stages of the sales chain, i.e. from the manufacturer or the importer. The amount of private copying compensation should be linked to the value of the creative works being copied, not to the price of the devices which can depend on commercial strategies. The private copying system should be brought into the digital age taking into account that consumers make private copies more than ever before on ever more connected devices and services. There is a need for common principles for defining applicable levy rates and devices/services that should be subject to levies. - See more at: http://www.directors.uk.com/europeancommissionguidelines#sthash.oI6qsZU7.dpuf ‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶. ‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶.

There are many differences accross borders in the EU which quite disbalance the markets. I.e. in Slovakia there is almost no income from copyright levies for the music indusrtry, while in Hungary, there is quite modest income from this. ‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶. ‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶‚Ä¶. Levies are still important in the digital world, particularly on storage devices. The small risk of ‚Äúdouble payments‚Äù does not outweigh the larger risk of no payments to authors and publishers. If fees are paid to different entities receiving different benefits from the work, this is not double payment unless the amount paid is, in both cases, for the same use/service. Levies are not the preferred option to compensate copyright owners but are the last resort where the work is on the market and the user is likely to make additional lawful uses of the material. Levies must not prevent or interfere with the contract between rightsholders and end users and are not meant to compensate for piracy.

ÔÇ YES‚ÄìPlease explain ÔÇ NO‚ÄìPlease explain Morover, The CJEU has already provided decisive interpretation regarding the scope and application of these exceptions (C-467/08 ‚Äì Padawan, C-462/09 ‚Äì Opus, C-457/11 ‚Äì Kyocera, C-521/11). Initiatives of the legislator are not required and would only disturb the ongoing harmonization process. Additional obligatory legislative tools are likely to harm this system. ÔÇ NO OPINION

ÔÇ YES‚ÄìPlease explain ÔÇ NO‚ÄìPlease explain Morover, The CJEU has already provided decisive interpretation regarding the scope and application of these exceptions (C-467/08 ‚Äì Padawan, C-462/09 ‚Äì Opus, C-457/11 ‚Äì Kyocera, C-521/11). Further judgments are awaited soon (eg C-435/12 ‚Äì ACI Adam). Under these circumstances, the CJEU provides the guidance required in the process of harmonization on EU level, including contemporaryunderstanding of the storage media to which these exceptions and levies in this context apply. The national courts follow this guidance, even if it takes time until cases dealing with these issues are finally decided. Initiatives of the legislator are not required and would only disturb the ongoing harmonization process. Over the years a successful system of remuneration of authors has been established in Austria which is firmly built on the private copy levy system. Additional obligatory legislative tools are likely to harm this system. ÔÇ NO OPINION

ÔÇ ‚ÄìPlease explain When a use is permitted by law and impactsarightsholderinour sector, it requires remuneration,and levies are one of the ways to remunerate. But no exceptionmayprejudice the normal exploitation of a work, even when compensated by a levy. Current levy systems, where in place, have their own merits and are one of the ways to foresee the compensation for private copying and reprography. In most cases, publishers are perfectly satisfied with their collective management organisationsand the levy system in place. However, some countries chose not to have levy systems and this should be respected.In Denmark we have very good experience with the Extended Collective Licensing Model.Indeed, every country deals with its situation within a national and cultural context which cannot be exported to the rest of Europe on an arbitrary basis. We therefore do not believe that there is currently a need to harmonise further the functioning of the levy systems.In particular, it must continue to be a requirement that certain exceptions are only permissible if fair compensation is provided to the rightholders. Rightholders eligible for a fair compensation comprise both the authors and the publishers. ÔÇ NO OPINION
